<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">polīticus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πολιτικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">politikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-icus</i>. First attested in 1629.
</p>

***politiek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a> (1977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">politique</i>. By analogy with Aristotle’s "τα πολιτικά" ('affairs of state').
</p>

***poltergeist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poltergeist.html>poltergeist</a> (63394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:poltergeist.html>Poltergeist</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">poltern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geist.html>Geist</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ghost</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:poltergeist.html>poltergeist</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">poltergeists</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">poltergeister</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An unseen ghost which <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> noises and causes disruption, especially by causing physical <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> to move or fly about.
<dl><dd><i>A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poltergeist.html>poltergeist</a></b> haunts the house by moving <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> around, making chain-rattling noises and throwing <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The chapel <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> haunted by a demonic <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poltergeist.html>poltergeist</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li>See also Thesaurus:ghost</li></ul>

***polygamie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:polygamie.html>polygamie</a> (53488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">polygamia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πολυγαμία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polugamía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pompelmoes.html>pompelmoes</a> (101150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain. Possibly from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pompoen.html>pompoen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pumpkin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pompel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big, swollen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">limoes</i>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:limoen.html>limoen</a></i> modeled after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">limões</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">citrus, <a href = vnd.unilang:lemons.html>lemons</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Another explanation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> as gradual corruption of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">pomo limões</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">citrus fruit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pompelmoes.html>pompelmoes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pompelmoes.html>pompelmoezen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pompelmoes.html>pompelmoesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pomelo <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit of the tree <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul">Citrus <a href = vnd.unilang:maxima.html>maxima</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***pond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pond</a> (1718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pont.html>pont</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pond</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*pundą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pound, weight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pondō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ponden.html>ponden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unit of mass, often broadly similar to 500 grams
<ol><li>metric pound <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">500 grams</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pondje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kopen.html>kopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:markt.html>markt</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> going to buy a <b>pound</b> (500 g) of cheese at the market.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperial units</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pound <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">453.6 grams</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pound, any of several local units, with a range between 420 and 500 grammes, divided into 16 historical ounces</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Dutch metric system</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kilogram</li></ol></li>
<li>one of several monetary units
<ol><li>British pound, pound sterling <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">currency</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ponden.html>ponden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vakantie.html>vakantie</a> in Wales.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I still have a few <b>pounds</b> left <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> from my holiday in Wales.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Egyptian pound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Flemish pound</li></ol></li></ol>

***pont.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pont.html>pont</a> (30304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ponte</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pontō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ferryboat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pōns</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pont.html>pont</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ponten.html>ponten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pont.html>pontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ferry, ferryboat</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veerpont.html>veerpont</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pont.html>pont</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***pooch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a> (40309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Of uncertain origin. One (unsubstantiated) conjecture <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that the word <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from <i>Putzi</i>, a common German name given to lapdogs.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> The name <i>Putzi</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possibly formed from German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Putz</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">-i</i>, influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">putzig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">funny, cute, small</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pooches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dog.</li>
<li>A dog of mixed breed; a mongrel.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably related to pouch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pooches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bulge, an enlarged part
<dl><dd><i>There's a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a></b> in the plastic where it got too hot.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A distended or swelled condition.
<dl><dd><i>Her left sleeve <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a></b> at the shoulder than the right.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pooches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pooching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pooched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To distend, to swell or extend beyond normal <a href = vnd.unilang:limits.html>limits</a>; usually used with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">out</i>.
<dl><dd><i>Inflate that tire too much and the tube may <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pooch.html>pooch</a></b> out of the cut in the sidewall.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1969</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_Angelou" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Maya Angelou"><a href = vnd.unilang:maya.html>Maya</a> Angelou</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/I_Know_Why_the_Caged_Bird_Sings" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:I Know Why the Caged Bird Sings">I Know Why the Caged Bird <a href = vnd.unilang:sings.html>Sings</a></a></i>, New York: Bantam, 1971, Chapter 21, p. 124,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/iknowwhycagedbi000maya">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> rustling <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a> from the <a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a> and the sides <b>pooched</b> out as if they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> trying to stand up.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">poke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pook.html>poken</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:pook.html>poken</a></i> (both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*puk-</i>), which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably imitative. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pose</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">pose</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pausa</i>.

***poot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a> (6174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pôte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">limb, claw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, further etymology unclear. The only known Germanic cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>pote</a></i>. Outside Germanic, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>pote</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca">pota</i> may be related.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pootje.html>pootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>limb (arm or <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>) of an animal (sometimes human)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spinnen.html>Spinnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:spiders.html>Spiders</a> have eight <b><a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> or foot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>Geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Not having a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></b> to stand on.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijf.html>Blijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Keep your <b>hands</b> off <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> of an object, e.g. furniture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruk.html>kruk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A stool with three <b><a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Although using <i><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></i> to denote limbs of humans in normally considered rude, there are some exceptions in case of idioms like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterste.html>achterste</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a>.</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">To get up on one's hind <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="4" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ruigpoot</i>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">popler</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">poplier</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">peuplier</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pōpulus</i>, with a suffix <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> added.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">poplars</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various deciduous trees of the genus <i>Populus</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Wood from the <a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a> tree.</li></ol>

***poppenkast.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poppenkast.html>poppenkast</a> (17989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pop</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">puppet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kast.html>kast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cupboard, casing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poppenkast.html>poppenkast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poppenkasten.html>poppenkasten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poppenkast.html>poppenkastje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A portable puppet theatre and <a href = vnd.unilang:puppets.html>puppets</a> for use in it.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">puppet-show</span>, notably of the Punch and Judy type.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bad, excessive or hilarious 'show', pointlessly <span class="Latn" lang="en">theatrical</span> conduct.</li></ol>

***populatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatie</a> (22450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">populātiō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">populare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to populate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">populus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a people, population</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populaties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A population, notably used in:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quantified presence of organisms on a territory</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">statistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any mass from which a sample can be drawn</li></ol></li></ol>

***populier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:populier.html>populier</a> (67982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">popelier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">poplier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pōpulus</i>. The spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> adapted to the Latin in the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a>, tree of the genus <i>Populus</i>.</li></ol>
